\bentry
\word[I(1)]{I, i}
\pron{ai}
\gl{\nA} (\bava\ \eng{Is} yA \eng{I's}). 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} iMgilxSf vaNaRmAleya oMbatatxneya akaSxra. 
\num{2} (roVmanf aMkanadalilx) = \eng{1;} `oMdu' 
\eng{(I, i = 1, ii = 2, ix = 9, cii = 102).}}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[I(2)]{I}
\pron{ai}
\gl{\sanA} (\bava\ \eng{we;}
\dictmeaning{ divxtiVyA viBakitx \eng{me} \ucAcx\ mi, yA otutx
hAkidAga mI; \AtAmx\ \eng{myself,} \pArxparx\ \eng{me}, \bava\ \eng{we;}
SaSiThxV viBakitx \eng{my, mine,} \bava\ \eng{our}). 
\num{1} \Eva\ \sanA\ parxthama puruSa \eng{me,} (\AmA);
(udAgxragaLalilx) \eng{ah me!, dear me!, silly me!}}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[ice(1)]{ice}
\pron{aisf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} aisu; niVgaRlulx; niVgaRDeDx; maMjugaDeDx; GaniVBavisida
niVru. 
\num{2} niVrina meVle teVluva maMjugaDeDxya hALe. 
\num{3} maMjugaDeDx
miThAyi yA adara tuMDu, \kanmu (\birx) aisfkirxVmf yA aisf peVDa. 
\num{4} (\ashi) vajarxgaLu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
{\dictmeaning{\eng{dry ice} Gana iMgAlada DeYAkesxYDu.}}

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{break the ice}
 
 
\alnum{a} AraMBa mADu; shuru mADu. 

 
\alnum{b} bigumAnavanunx biDu; shirxVmadAgxMBiVyaRvanunx tore. 
\num{2} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{cut(2) nuga(21)}{${}^2$cuts} no ice.} 
\num{3} \eng{on ice} 

 
\alnum{a} (ATa, vinoVda, \mo vugaLa \vi) (himatalada
meVle) jArugaru, sekxVTarugaLu-mADida. 

 
\alnum{b} (\AmA) tAtAkxlikavAgi-sathxgitagoLisiruva, nilugaDeyalilx(TiTx)ruva, taDehiDidiruva. 
 
\alnum{c} (\AmA) KaDAKaMDitavAda; KacitavAda. 
\hyperdef{I}{ice(1) nuga(4)}{}
\num{4} \eng{on thin ice} atisUkaSxmX parisithxtiyalilx; aBadarx sithxtiyalilx;
apAyadalilx: \eng{you are on thin ice with that argument} A vAdavanunx
hiDidare ninanx sithxti aBadarx.} 
\eentry

\bentry
\word{idea}
\pron{aiDia}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} Adi yA ASaR parxtiVka; mUla mAdari; sutatxla parxpaMcadalilx
nAvu kANuva yAvudeV vagaRda nijiRVva yA sajiVva vasutxvina lakaSxNagaLiMda
BinanxvAgidudx A vagaRda AdashaR lakaSxNagaLanunx hoMdideyenanxlAda, A 
vagaRda mUla mAdari yA ASeRVya parxtiVka.
\num{2} (guriyAgiTuTxkoLaLxbeVkAdudu,
saqSiTxsabeVkAdudu, \mo vugaLa) kalapxne; BAvane; AloVcane. 
\num{3} udedxVsha;
aBipArxya; yoVjane: \eng{the idea of becoming an engineer} eMjiniyarAgabeVkeMba
udedxVsha. 
\num{4} manoVBAvane; manasisxge hoLeda kalapxne. 
\num{5} AloVcanA
vidhAna; AloVcaneya-mAgaR, riVti, dhoVraNe. 
\num{6} kalapxne; (asapxSaTx)
BAvane; eNike: \eng{the idea of his doing such a thing} avanu iMtha kelasa
mADuvaneMba eNike. \eng{I had no idea you were there} niVnu alilxruve eMba
kalapxneyeV nanagiralilalx. 
\num{7} (pelxVToVvina tatatxvX) AdashaR rUpa;
yAva vagaRdalAlxdarU iruva parxteyxVka vasutxgaLu yAvudara apUNaR parxtigaLAgiruvuvoV A cirasAthxyiyAda AdashaR rUpa. 
\num{8} (DeVkATfR, lAkf ivara sidAdhxMtagaLalilx yA mAnasika arivina) parxtayxkaSx viSaya. 
\num{9} (kAYxMTf) parAsatetx; anuBavAtiVtavAda matutx ciMtanada shudadhx takaRkekx mAtarx goVcaravAda viSaya. 
\num{10} (hegelf) (vAyxvahArika satayxvelalxvU yAvudara aBivayxkitxyoV A)
pAramAthiRka satayx.}}

 \noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{have no idea} (\AmA) 
 
\alnum{a} gotetxVilalxdiru. 
 
\alnum{b} tiVra asamathaRnAgiru. 
\num{2} \eng{get (\engit{or} have) ideas}
(\AmA) heVrAse, avidheVyate, \mo vanunx uLaLxvanAgiru. 
\num{3} \eng{man
of ideas} parxtuyxtapxnanxmati; samayasUPxtiRyuLaLxvanu. 
\num{4} \eng{not my idea of} (\AmA) nAnu aMdukoLuLxvaMthadadxlalxda;
nananx kalapxneyadadxlalxda: \eng{this is not my idea of a pleasant
evening} idu nananx kalapxneya hitavAda saMjeyalalx.
\num{5} \eng{put ideas into person's head} obabxna(La) talege
hiriyAse \mo vanunx tuMbu; obabxnige taMtAne bArade iruvaMtaha mahadAkAMkeSx
\mo vanunx sUcisu; (mahatAvxkAMkeSx \mo) BAvanegaLanunx talege tuMbu. 
\num{6} \eng{that's an idea} (\AmA) A sUcane (\mo dudx) parishiVlanAhaRvAgide. 
\num{7} \eng{the big idea} (\sA\ vayxMgayxvAgi) mahAyoVjane; GanoVdedxVsha: \eng{what's
the big idea?} EnayAyx adu, GanoVdedxVsha? (Enadu hucAcxTa! eMbathaRdalilx).
\hypertarget{idea nuga8}{}
\num{8} \eng{the very idea!} AhA! eMtha kalapxne! sUcane! (\AmA)
(asamamxti yA BinAnxBipArxyavanunx sUcisuva udAgxra).
\num{9} \eng{the young idea} eLeya manasusx; maguvina manasusx. 
\num{10} \eng{what an idea!} = \hyperlink{idea nuga8}{\nuga $(8)$}.}

\num{3} oNa; shuSakx; baraDu; kelasakekx bArada; nirupayukatx: \eng{idle chatter} kADuharaTe; kelasakekx bArada
haraTe. 
\num{4} (manuSayxra \vi) kelasavilalxda; nirudoyxVgi; udoyxVgavilalxda.

hALubidadx; pALubidadx: \eng{idle tenements} vAsavilalxda nivAsagaLu. \eng{idle capital} duDiyada baMDavALa; anutApxdaka baMDavALa. 
\num{6} soVmAriyAda; meYgaLaLxnAda: \eng{idle boys in the street} biVdiyalilxya meYgaLaLx huDugaru.
\num{7} baLasutitxlalxda; niSikxrXya; kelasa mADutitxlalxda: \eng{idle machinery} kelasa mADutitxlalxda yaMtarx. 
\num{8} (kAla \mo vugaLa \vi) kelasavirada; virAmada.

\bentry
\word[if(1)]{if}
\pron{iphf}
\gl{\saMavayx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} -re; -idadxre; -idadxlilx; -Adalilx; -pakaSxkekx; -pakaSxdalilx: \eng{if you are tired} niVnu baLalidadxre. \eng{if you (hereafter) see him,
give him the message} avanu ninage (muMde) sikakxre I sudidx koDu. 
\num{2} (asaMBavavAda saMdaBaRvanunx sUcisuvalilx yAvudeV dhAtuvina BUtarUpadoDane)
 -- oMdu veVLe Adare, idadxre, naDedare: \eng{if I were you} nAneV niVnAgididxdadxre; ninanx sAthxnadalilx yA sithxtiyalilx nAnu ididxdadxre. \eng{if he came
tomorrow} nALe avanu oMdu veVLe baMdare. 
\num{3} yAvAga; eMdAdarU; yAvAgalAdarU: \eng{if I feel any doubt} yAvAgalAdarU nanage saMshaya baMdare. 
\num{4} -yoV; -yeV; -vudeV; sAdhayxveV: \eng{see if you can turn the handle} hiDiyanunx
tirugisalu ninage AgutatxdeyeV noVDu. 
\num{5} 
\alnum{a} \eng{if} padavanunx
biTuTxbiTATxga kirxyApadavu kataqR padakekx modaleV barutatxde, \udA:
\eng{were in your place (= if I were in your place). would, could, should,
might, had he (= if he would, could, should, might, had).} 
 
\alnum{b} (\kAparx) \eng{loved I not honour more = if I loved not honour more.} 
\num{6} (bayake, AshacxyaR, \mo vugaLa udAgxragaLalilx vAkayxda anugata BAgavilalxde):
\eng{if I only knew!} nanage tiLididadxre (eSuTx cenAnxgitutx)!
\eng{if I haven't lost my watch!} nananx gaDiyAravanunx nAnu
kaLedukoLaLxdidadxre! (kaLedukoMDenalAlx eMba AshacxyaRda yA beVsarada
dhavxni).
\num{7} (vinayadiMda beVDuvAga) \eng{if you wouldn't mind opening the door?} niVnu EnU tiLidukoLaLxdidadxre dayamADi bAgilu tegeyuveyA? 
\num{8} AdarU; hAgidadxrU; AdAgUyx: \eng{a useful if cumbersome
device} toDakinadAdarU upayukatx salakaraNe.}}

 \noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{as if} -hAge; -aMte; -heVgoV hAge: \eng{it seems as if
he meant} (ADumAtinalilx \eng{means} eMdu \parx) \eng{to compromise} avanige
rAjimADikoLuLxva aBipArxyavidadx hAge toVrutatxde. \eng{he talks as if he
were drunk} avanu kuDididadxre heVge mAtanADutitxdadxnoV hAge (yA kuDididadxre
heVgoV hAge) mAtanADutAtxne. \eng{as if you didn't know} ninage EnU
gotitxlalxdidadxMte (ninage cenAnxgi gotutx eMba dhavxni).
\num{2} \eng{if and when} (Aguva saMBavavidadxre) AdAga; hAgAdAga; muMde; BaviSayxdalilx. 
\hypertarget{if nuga3}{}
\num{3} \eng{if any} yAvudAdarU yA yAvuvAdarU idadxlilx. 
\num{4} \eng{if anything} = \hyperlink{if nuga3}{\nuga $(3)$}. 
\num{5} \eng{if at all} 
 
\alnum{a} pArxyashaH ilalxveV ilalx. 
 
\alnum{b} aMtAdarU, hAgAdarU -- ilalx. 
\num{6} \eng{if not} hAgiradidadxre; aMtiradidadxlilx. 
\hypertarget{if nuga7}{}
\num{7} \eng{if only because} (beVre yAvudeV kAraNakAkxgi AgadidadxrU) A kAraNakAkxgi; adakAkxgi. 
\num{8} \eng{if only to} = \hyperlink{if nuga7}{\nuga $(7)$}. 
\hypertarget{if nuga9}{}

\bentry
\word{illustrate}
\pron{ilaseTxrXVTf}
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} sapxSaTxpaDisu; vivarisu; vishadagoLisu: \eng{illustrated the new theory by references to what was already known} AgaleV gotitxdadx viSayada
ulelxVKagaLa mUlaka hosa sidAdhxMtavanunx vivarisidanu. 
\num{2} udAharaNe koDu;
daqSATxMta koDu; nidashiRsu; udAharaNegaLiMda sapxSaTxpaDisu: \eng{gave many
examples to illustrate his lecture} tananx upanAyxsavanunx sapxSaTx paDisalu
aneVka udAharaNegaLanunx niVDidanu. 
\num{3} (vaNaRne \mo vanunx) sacitarxvAgi
vivarisu; (reVKA) citarxgaLiMda vishadiVkarisu: \eng{an illustrated textbook}
sacitarx paThayxpusatxka. 
\num{4} (pusatxka, vataRmAnapatirxke, \mo vanunx)
citirxVkarisu; citarxgaLiMda alaMkarisu, aMdagoLisu.}}

 \noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} udAharisu: udAharaNeyAgu; nidashaRnavAgu; daqSATxMtavAgu:

manoVBAvavanunx udAharisutatxde.

vivarisu: \eng{to prevent misunderstanding, let me illustrate} tapupx garxhikeyanunx tapipxsalu -- udAharaNe koDutetxVne, udAharaNegaLiMda vivarisutetxVne.}

\bentry
\word{imbricative}
\pron{iMbirxkaTivf}
\gl{\gu}
\dictmeaning{heMcu hodikeyaMtha; oMdara meVloMdaraMte hodisiruva heMcugaLaMtiruva
poregaLiMda mucicxda yA mADida.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{imbroglio}
\pron{iMborxVloyxV}
\gl{\nA} (\bava\ \eng{imbroglios}). 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} asatxvayxsatx rAshi; celAlxpililx
bididxruva rAshi: \eng{an imbroglio of papers and books} celAlxpililxyAgi
bididxruva kAgadagaLa matutx pusatxkagaLa rAshi. 
\num{2} (\kanmu\ rAjakiVyadalilx yA nATakadalilx) toDaku (saMdaBaR); asatxvayxsatxte; bikakxTuTx; mugagxTuTx;
jaTila parisithxti; goVTALi: \eng{the play is clever in its intrigue and
imbroglio} nATakavu tananx pitUri matutx jaTila saninxveVshagaLiMda camatAkxravAgide. 
\num{3} (vayxkitxgaLa yA deVshagaLa madheyx uMTAguva toDakina yA kahiya)
manasAtxpa; BinAnxBipArxya: \eng{an imbroglio between foreign ministers}
videVshAMga maMtirxgaLa naDuvaNa manasAtxpa.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{imbrue}
\pron{iMbUrx}
\gl{\sakirx}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (tananx keY, katitx, \mo vanunx rakatxdiMda, koleyiMda) kalegoLisu; kaLaMkagoLisu; kaluSitagoLisu; kaLaMkita mADu: \eng{these hands in murder are imbrued} I keYgaLu koleyiMda kaLaMkitavAgive. 
\num{2} toVyisu; nenasu;
sikatxgoLisu: \eng{a nation imbrued with the blood of executed men} galilxgeVrisalapxTaTx janara rakatxdiMda toyudxhoVda rASaTxrX.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{immediate}
\pron{imIDiaTf}
\gl{\gu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (vayxkitx yA vasutxvige matotxMdaroDane iruva saMbaMdhada 
\vi) neVra; parxtayxkaSx; sAkASxtAtxda; madhayxvatiRyilalxda; naDuve EnU
ilalxda; avayxvahita: \eng{the immediate cause of death} sAvina parxtayxkaSx kAraNa. 
\num{2} (saMbaMdhada yA kirxyeya \vi) neVravAda; sAkASxtf;
madhayxvatiRyilalxda; samakaSx: \eng{they rest upon the immediate testimony
of consciousness} avu ceVtanada neVravAda rujuvAtanunx avalaMbisive. 
\num{3} ati samiVpada; atayxMta nikaTavAda; nereya; magugxlina; pakakxda: \eng{my
immediate neighbour} nananx magugxlina nereyavanu. 
\num{4} tatfkaSxNada; tutARda; jarUrAda; oDaneyeV saMBavisuva; kUDaleV naDeyuva; taDavilalxda:
\eng{an immediate reply} taDavilalxda utatxra; oDaneyeV koTaTx javAbu. \eng{our
immediate concern was to get him to hospital} avananunx Asapxterxge oyuyxvudu
namamx tutuR kelasavAgitutx. 
\num{5} (jAcnxnada \vi) neVravAda; parxtayxkaSxvAda; aparoVkaSx; takaRda neravilalxde paDeda.}

jAcnxnasAnxna mADisuvudu.

maganxte; muLugiruvudu.

inonxMdara hiMde yA inonxMdara neraLinalilx mareyAguvudu.}

\bentry
\word[implement(1)]{implement}
\pron{iMpilxmaMTf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (piVThoVpakaraNa, uDupu, \mo) sAmagirx; sAmAnu. 
\num{2} (\bava dalilx) (piVThoVpakaraNa, uDupu, \mo vugaLa) sajujx.

 \noindent
\gl{\pagu}

\bentry
\word[imprint(2)]{imprint}
\pron{iMpirxMTf}
\gl{\sakirx}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (citarx \mo vugaLa) muderxyotutx; acocxtutx; Thasesxyotutx.
\num{2} (BAvane \mo vanunx) manasisxna -- meVle acocxtutx, nATisu, muderxyotutx;
manadaTuTx mADu. 
\num{3} (yAvudeV vasutxvina yA vayxkitxya meVle avugaLa yoVgayxte, guNa, \mo vanunx) muderxyotutx; acocxtutx. 
\num{4} (vasutxvina meVle)
citarx otutx; citarxda gurutu hAku. 
\num{5} (\mashA) ApatxvAgu; pirxya(vasutx)vAgu; \kanmu\ eLeya pArxNige Apatx yA pirxyabaMdhuveMdu toVruvaMte Agu:
\eng{the parent fish may become imprinted to the young as well as the young
to the parent} tAyimInu marige ApatxvAgabahudAdaMteyeV mariyU tAyige Agabahudu.
\num{6} (\mashA) ApatxvAgisu; pirxyavasutxvAgisu; \kanmu\ eLeya mariyoMdu beVroMdu pArxNiyanunx yA vasutxvanunx tananx Apatx yA pirxyabaMdhuvAgi kANuvaMte
ogigxsu: \eng{we took ducklings from their natural mother and tried to
imprint them to humans} bAtina marigaLanunx hetatx tAyiyiMda biDisi avugaLige
manuSayxranunx ApatxvAgisidevu.}
\eentry

\word[in(2)]{in}
\pron{inf}
\gl{\kirxvi}
{\dictmeaning{(kelavu elelxgaLa oLagiruva sAthxnavanunx yA aMtha
sAthxnakekx calanavanunx sUcisuva \kirxvi vAgi).
\num{1} (koVNe, mane, AvaraNa, \mo vugaLa)
oLage; oLagaDe; oLakekx; -- alilx: \eng{come in} oLage bA. \eng{send
him in} avananunx oLakekx kaLuhisu. \eng{walk in} (oLakekx) bA.
\num{2} maneyalilx; gaqhadalilx; \kanmu\ savxgaqhadalilx, tananx maneyalilx: \eng{he is in} avanu 
maneyalilxdAdxne. \eng{will be in tomorrow} nALe maneyalilxrutAtxre.
\num{3} patirxkeyalilx; patirxkeyoLage: \eng{put a notice in} patirxkeyalilx
oMdu parxkaTaNe hAku. \eng{is my article in?} nananx leVKana patirxkeyalilx
baMdideyeV? \eng{looked for the word, but it was not in} A padakAkxgi
huDukide, Adare adu pusatxkadalilxralilalx. 
\num{4} oLage; oLagaDe; oLaBAgadalilx: \eng{coat with the woolly side
in} tupapxTa BAga oLameYyalilxruva, oLagaDeyiruva -- aMgi.
\num{5} (oMdu vasutxvanunx) sututxgaTiTx; Avarisi; mutitx; mucicx;
digabxMdhanadalilxrisi; oLage iTuTx: \eng{hemmed in} beVliyiMda
sututxgaTiTx. \eng{locked in} oLage kUDi biVga hAki. \eng{walled in} sutatx
goVDeyiMda Avarisi. \eng{cover in} oLage seVrisi mucicxbiDu. \eng{roof
in} cAvaNi hAku; cAvaNiyiMda mucucx. 
\num{6} (phAyxSanf, baLake, kAla, adhikAra, pariNAmakAriyAda yA
anukUlakara kirxye) iruvaMte; baMdiruvaMte; odagiruvaMte: \eng{short
skirts are in} kirulaMgagaLu Iga phAYxSanf Agive. \eng{mangoes are
in} mAvina haNuNxgaLa kAla baMdide. \eng{the Liberals are in} libaralf pakaSxdavaru adhikArakekx baMdidAdxre. \eng{my luck was in} nananx adaqSaTxda kAla
odagitutx. 
\num{7} (bAyxTugAra, cunAyita aBayxthiR, \mo varaMte) vatiRsi;
naDedukoMDu: \eng{before he had been five minutes in} (kirxkeTf) avanu
ATakikxLida aidu nimiSadoLagAgi; avanu bAyxTu mADatoDagida aidu nimiSadoLage.
\num{8} (maneya uriya \vi) uriyutitxruvaMte: \eng{keep the fire in} beMkiyanunx uriyutatxleV, uriyuvaMte -- iTiTxru. 
\num{9} (reYlu, doVNi, kAla, sugigx, koVrike, \mo vugaLa \vi) 

\alnum{a} baMdiruvaMte; talupiruvaMte. 
 
\alnum{b} sivxVkarisuvaMte. 
\num{10} (\uparx daMte) bahujana oMdugUDi diVGaRkAlika yA satatavAgi mADuva
kAyaRkarxmavanunx sUcisuvalilx: \eng{sit-in} beYThakf muSakxra; kelasa nililxsi
bahujana kuLitu naDesuva muSakxra. \eng{teach-in} bahujana oMdugUDi naDesuva
shikaSxNa. 
\num{11} (\sakirx gaLoDane) BeVdisikoMDu oLahokukx, oLahoVgi:
\eng{burn in} kAyisi (inonxMdaroDane) bese. \eng{cut in} koredu kUDisu.\eng{rub in} 

 
\alnum{a} ujijx oLahogisu; ujijx oLakekx parxveVshisuvaMte mADu.

 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) (apirxyavAdadadxnunx heVLi heVLi) manasasxnunx -- cucucx, kututx.}}

\bentry
\word[indeed(1)]{indeed}
\pron{infDiVDf}
\gl{\kirxvi}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} satayxvAgi; diTavAgi; nijakUkx; nishacxyavAgi; vAsatxvavAgi:
\eng{he was, indeed, a remarkable man} nishacxyavAgi avanu asAdhAraNa manuSayx.
\num{2} (visheVSavAgi otitx heVLuvAga) nijavAgiyU; diTavAgiyU; satayxvAgiyU:
\eng{I shall be very glad indeed} nijavAgiyU nanage tuMbA saMtoVSa. \eng{this is quick work indeed} diTavAgiyU idu curukAda kelasa. \eng{indeed it is}
nijavAgiyU adeV. \eng{yes, indeed} hwdu, nija. 
\num{3} (satAyxMshavanunx heVLuvalilx) nijavAgi; vAsatxvavAgi: \eng{if indeed such a thing is possible} nijavAgi aMtha oMdu viSaya sAdhayxvAda pakaSxdalilx. \eng{saw here recently, indeed
yesterday} ititxVcege noVDide, nijavAgi nenenx. 
\num{4} (obabxra mAtanunx
samathiRsuvAga yA vayxMgayxvAgi nirAkarisuvAga) nijavAgi: \eng{who is this
Mr.\ Rao? who is he, indeed!} I rAvf yAru? nijavAgi, avaru yAru! (hAgeMdu
keVLabahudeV ?) 
\num{5} (mAtina athaRda oMdu aMshavanunx opipxkoLuLxvAga)
nijavAgi: \eng{there are indeed exceptions} apavAdagaLive, nija. 
\num{6} (parxshAnxthaRkavAgi) hwdeV ? hAgeyeV? nijaveV? : \eng{``that's Ram.''
``Indeed?''} ``avanu rAma.'' ``hwdeV?''}
\eentry

tuMbi) ubibxda sithxti.

\bentry

hudugiruva guhe.

\num{2} (BAvaneyanunx) paroVkaSxvAgi tiLisuvaMte; vayxMjaneya mUlaka sUcisuva riVtiyalilx.}
\eentry

\bentry

\pron{infsinuyxESanf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (\kanmu\ hiVnayisuva riVtiya) paroVkaSx yA rahasayx sUcane:
 \eng{nasty insinuations about his rival} tananx parxtisapxdhiRyanunx
 hiVnayisuva paroVkaSx sUcanegaLu. 
\num{2} rahasayxvAda yA kuyukitxya sUcane, suLivu: \eng{his methods of
 insinuation are ingenious} avana kuyukitxya sUcanAriVtigaLu
 caturavAdavu.
\num{3} (sUkaSxmXvAgi yA kuyukitxyiMda) manasasxnunx tuMbuvudu.
\num{4} (vayxkitxya pirxVti, vishAvxsa, anugarxha saMpAdanege)
 anunaya; hosedukoMDu hoVguvike; majiRhiDiyuvike; pusalAvaNe;
 anugarxha saMpAdane: \eng{he made his way by flattery and
 insinuation} hogaLike pusalAvaNegaLa mUlaka avanu muMdebaMda.

\num{3} (\kanmu\ muKaBAvada \vi) utusxka; sharxdAdhxpUvaRka; tiVvArxBilASeya; kutUhalada; AsakitxyiMda tuMbiruva.}
\eentry


\bentry

BAvanegaLu; Adayx kalapxnegaLu (\udA\ mara, hasu itAyxdi).

mAyuvike; netatxru hepupxgaTiTx gAya mAyuvudu; gAyada meVle
keMpukaNagaLu rUpugoMDu avugaLa neraviniMda camaR seVrikoMDu gAya
mAyuvudu.
\num{5} \eng{second intentions} (parxthama BAvaneya meVle

vayxtAyxsa, jAti, guNa, \mo vu).

\bentry
\word{into}
\pron{iMTu(Ta)}
\gl{\upa} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (\rUpa\ saha) (oMdu vasutxvina, oMdu biMduvina kaDege calaneya
dikakxnunx toVrisuvAga) oLakekx; oLagaDege; aMtaH -- : \eng{come into
the garden} toVTadoLakekx bA. \eng{throw it into the fire} beMkige
bisADu.
$4$ \eng{(divided) into} $20=5$ nAlAkxgi viBAgisida $20=5$.
\num{2} (badalAvaNe, sithxti, pariNAma -- ivanunx tiLisuvAga)
oMdakekx; rUpakekx; rUpavAgi: \eng{turn stones into gold}
kalulxgaLanunx cinanxkekx, honinxge -- tirugisu. \eng{translate into
English} iMgilxSige BASAMtarisu. \eng{grow into an adult} vayasakxnAgi
beLe. \eng{collect them into heaps} avanunx rAshigaLAgi
sheVKarisu. \eng{divide them into three classes} avanunx mUru
vagaRgaLAgi viBAgisu. \eng{flogged into submission} sharaNAguvaMte,
sharaNAguvavaregU koraDiniMda baDidu.
\num{3} (\AmA) Asakitxyiruva; tiLidiruva: \eng{is really into art}
nijavAgiyU kaleyalilx Asakitxyide.}}

 \noindent 
\gl{\nuga}
\dictmeaning{

\num{5} \eng{look into the matter} I viSayavanunx parishiVlisu.

\bentry
\word{introduction}
\pron{infTarxDakfSanf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} parxveVshana; oLage, oLakekx taruvudu. 
\num{2} aMtaniRveVshana; oLage, oLakekx iDuvudu, seVrisuvudu; oLahogisuvudu. 
\num{3} oLakekx seVrisida -- vasutx, viSaya. 
\num{4} (padadhxti, BAvane, sudhAraNe, \mo vanunx) baLakege, AcaraNege taruvudu; cAlitxgoLisuvudu. 
\num{5} (viSaya \mo vanunx) muMdiDuvudu; muMdoDuDxvudu; sUcisuvudu; maMDisuvudu; maMDane. 
\num{6} (pusatxka, BASaNa, \mo vugaLa pArxraMBadalilx mADuva yA seVrisuva) parxsAtxvane; upoVdAvxta; BUmike; piVThike; viSayada paricaya. 
\num{7} keYpiDi; viSayavanunx paricaya mADikoDuva pArxthamika garxMtha. 
\num{8} (obabxnanunx inonxbabxnige) vidhuyxkatxvAgi paricaya mADikoDuvudu; vidhuyxkatx paricaya, sAMparxdAyika paricaya. 
\num{9} (variSaThxvagaRda taruNiyanunx) ADhayx samAjakekx paricayisuvudu, parxveVshagoLisuvudu. 
\num{10} (masUde \mo vanunx) shAsanasaBeyalilx -- maMDisuvudu;
maMDane. 
\hypertarget{introduction(11)}{}
\num{11} paricaya patarx.}}

 \noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\eng{letter of introduction =
\hyperlink{introduction(11)}{introduction(11)}.}}

\bentry

\dictmeaning{

\num{2} tirugumurugu; vipayaRya; vayxtayxya; sAthxna, karxma, saMbaMdha -- ivu hiMdu muMdAgiruvudu. 
\num{3} (\kanmu\ vAyxkaraNada padakarxmadalilx, AlaMkArika
pariNAmakAkxgi) karxmavayxtayxya; padakarxma, shabadx -- vipayaRya
(\udA\ \eng{how beautiful is the rose} eMbalilx kataqRpada
vipayaRyavAgide).
\num{4} (\ga) viloVmakirxye; viloVmakaraNa; viloVma mADuvudu; (yAvudeV parxmANavanunx) hiMdumuMdu mADuvudu. 
\num{5} (\saM) 
 
\alnum{a} viloVmakirxye; savxra -- vayxtayxya, vipayaRya; AroVhaNa karxmadalilxruva savxragaLanunx avaroVhaNa karxmakekx yA avaroVhaNadalilxruvudanunx AroVhaNa karxmakekx taruvudu. 
 
\alnum{b} hAge mADidudx. 
\num{6} saliMgakAmukate. 
\num{7} viloVmana: 
 
\alnum{a} (\pashA) aunanxtayxdoMdige tApa vayxtAyxsavAguva karxma hiMdumuMdAguvike. 
 
\alnum{b} (\ravi) dhurxviVkaqta beLakina dhurxviVkaraNa samatala eDakekx tirugutitxdudxdu balakekx yA balakekx tirugutitxdudxdu eDakekx tiruguvudu. 
 
\alnum{c} (\ravi) (kabibxna sakakxre kuritaMte) jalaviBajane hoMdi gUlxkoVsf matutx pharxkoTxVsfgaLa misharxNavAguvudu.}

\dictmeaning{ayoDinf:

kapupx saPxTikagaLanunx matutx neVriLe baNaNxda AviyanUnx rUpisuva,
auSadhi matutx CAyAcitarxNagaLalilx baLasuva, jiVvigaLa atayxgatayx
aMshavAgiruva, hAyxlojanf guMpige seVrida aloVha dhAtu, \saMkeV\
\eng{I}.
 
\alnum{b} tiVkaSxNXvalalxda pUtinAshakavAgi (\eng{antiseptic})
baLasuva, AlakxhAlinalilx mADida ayoDinf dArxvaNa.}

 kareyuva, raMdharx uLaLx, beVkeMdAga higugxva matutx kugugxva
 sAmathayxRviruva pore.
 
\alnum{b} iriDeVsiV vaMshakekx seVrida, padamxpuSakxra eMba
 sasayxvanonxLagoMDa, geDeDx sahitavAda sasayxgaLa kula.
 
\alnum{c} oLagiruva siVLikegaLa pariNAmavAgi vividha baNaNxgaLanunx
 toVruva kAvxTfsxR haraLu. 
\hypertarget{iris(d)}{}
 
\alnum{d} sinimA kAyxmaragaLalilx oLahoguva beLakina parxmANavanunx
niyaMtirxsalu baLasuva oMdu bageya pore.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[iron(1)]{iron}
\pron{aianfR}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (\ravi) kabibxNa; ayasusx (\saMkeV\ \eng{Fe}). 
\num{2} (\rUpa) dADhayxR; kAThinayx; sethxyXyaR; bagagxdiruvike:
\eng{a man of iron} ukikxnaMtha manuSayx; kaTATxLu; sethxYyaRshAli.
\num{3} kabibxNada -- sAdhana, upakaraNa, hatAyxra: \eng{curling iron}
guMguru haNige; kuruLu haNige; kUdalanunx guMguru mADalu baLasuva
sAdhana.
\num{4} isitxrX peTiTxge. 
\num{5} (kabibxNada taleyuLaLx) gAlfphx dAMDu. 
\num{6} (\bava dalilx) beVDi; koVLa; saMkoVle. 
\num{7} (\sA\ \bava dalilx) rikApu. 
\num{8} (\bava dalilx) (kabibxNada) kAlukaTuTx; pAdabaMdhani; aMgavikAra saripaDisalu hAkuva kAlukaTuTx. 
\num{9} (kabibxNada dhAtuviniMda tayArisida) TAnikukx; shakitxvadhaRka auSadhi: \eng{iron tablets} kabibxNada guLigegaLu. 
\num{10} (\ashi) pisUtxlu. 
\num{11} (baDagiya) hatatxriya alagu. 
\num{12} (timiMgalada beVTege baLasuva) kabibxNada ITi. 
\num{13} (\pArxparx) katitx; KaDagx. 
\num{14} kabibxNada baregoVlu; barehAkuva, muderxyotutxva kaDiDx, kaMb, koVlu, \mo vu.}}

\gl{\pagu}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{cast iron} tAMDavALa; erakada kabibxNa; sheVkaDa $2$riMda $4.5$raSuTx kAbaRnf matutx $1$riMda $4$raSuTx silikanf uLaLx, matutx erakakekx anukUlavAda oMdu vidhada kabibxNa.

\num{3} \eng{rod of iron} kUrxravAda, kaThinavAda riVti: \eng{rule with a rod of iron} kaThinavAgi ALu. 
\hyperdef{I}{iron(1) nuga(4)}{}

\bentry
\word[irony(1)]{irony}
\pron{airani}
\gl{\nA} (\bava\ \eng{ironies}). 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} kaTaki; vayxMgayx; aNaka; airani; \kanmu\ obabxna aBipArxya
alalxgaLeyalu, adanenxV opupxvaMte naTisi mAtanADi virudAdhxBipArxya
sUcisuvudu yA hAge sUcisida mAtu. 
\hypertarget{irony(1)2}{}
\num{2} (vidhi, dashe, \mo vugaLa) duGaRTane; duviRdhi; asaMgata
GaTane; vidhiya aNaka; vidhi viDaMbana; sahajavAgi
apeVkaSxNiVyavAgidudx, hitakAraka daqSiTxyiMdaloV eMbaMte toVridarU
nijavAgi devxVSAsUyegaLiMda kUDidudx, akAladalilx asaMgatavAgi
saMBavisuva duGaRTane.

\bentry
\word[isolate(1)]{isolate}
\pron{aisaleVTf}
\gl{\sakirx}

\bentry
\word[issue(1)]{issue}
\pron{iSU(sUyx)}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (huMDi, baMDavALa patarxgaLu, kAgadada haNa, sATxMpugaLu, \mo vanunx) horaDisuvudu; parxcAlana; niVDike. 
\num{2} omemx horaDisida nANayxgaLu, kAgadada haNa, vaqtatxpatirxkeya parxtigaLu, \mo vugaLa motatx, saMKeyx. 
\num{3} (pusatxka) saMcike; nidiRSaTx kAlAvadhiyalilx visheVSAMshagaLanonxLagoMDu parxkaTavAguva Avaqtitxya BAga (saMcike): \eng{May issue} meV saMcike. 
\num{4} koTaTx yA haMcida -- vasutx yA motatx: \eng{issue of rations}
reVSaninxna niVDike yA haMcike. 
\hypertarget{issue(1)5}{}
\num{5} horahoraDuvudu; hora harita; horasurita; nigaRmana; bahigaRmana; nisasxraNa; niSakxrXmaNa: \eng{the issue of water from a broken pipe} oDeda koLaveyiMda niVrina surita. 
\num{6} horadAri; niSakxrXma; nigaRma; horakekx hoVguva mAgaR: \eng{a labyrinth that had no issue} horakekx hoVguva mAgaRvilalxda cakarxBiVmana koVTe. 
\num{7} (nadi \mo vugaLa) ugama sAthxna; horabaruva sathxLa. 
\num{8} (nadi, aMtadeRVshiVya samudarx, \mo vugaLa) muKa; horahariyuva, biVLuva jAga. 
\num{9} (kirxye \mo vugaLa) mugita; mukAtxya; samApitx; kone; aMtayx: \eng{negotiations were brought to an issue} saMdhAnagaLanunx mukAtxyakekx taralAyitu. 
\num{10} PalitAMsha; pariNAma; Pala: \eng{the issue of a contest} sapxdheRya PalitAMsha. 
\num{11} (\nAyxshA) makakxLu; saMtAna; saMtati: \eng{without male issue} gaMDu saMtAnavilalxde. 
\num{12} (\pArxparx) (rakatx \mo vugaLa) sArxva; osaru; harivu; soVrike; surita: \eng{an issue of blood from the nose} mUginiMda rakatxsArxva. 
\num{13} (rakatx \mo vanunx) sarxvisalu mADida kacucx, gAya. 
\num{14} (\kanmu\ \nAyxshA) (eraDu pakaSxgaLa naDuve niNaRyisabeVkAda) vivAdAMsha; vAdaviSaya.}}

 \noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{at issue} 
 
\alnum{a} (vayxkitxgaLa \vi) BinAnxBipArxyavuLaLxvarAgi; omamxtavilalxdavarAgi: \eng{for years they remained at issue with each other} vaSaRgaTaTxle avaru tamomxLage BinAnxBipArxyavuLaLxvarAgidadxru. 
 
\alnum{b} (vasutxgaLa \vi) vAdagarxsatxvAda; vivAdAsapxdavAda; caceRgoLapaTiTxruva: \eng{the question at issue is whether the majority opinion is always right} bahumatABipArxya yAvAgalU sariyeV eMba parxshenx vivAdAsapxda. 
\num{2} \eng{force the issue} niNaRyavanunx otAtxyisu; tiVmARna talupuvaMte balavaMta mADu. 
\num{3} \eng{in the issue} hAgAdAga; saMdaBaR odagidaMte; parisithxti
hAgAdAga.
\num{4} \eng{issue of fact} vAsatxva saMgatiyanunx kurita vivAdAMsha. 
\num{5} \eng{issue of law} kAnUnanunx kurita vivAdAMsha. 
\hypertarget{issue1 pagu6}{} \hyperdef{I}{issue(1) pagu(6)}{}
\num{6} \eng{join issue} 
 
\alnum{a} (vivAdAMshaveMdu opipxda viSayada meVle, inonxbabxroDane)
vAdakekx -- iLi, toDagu, AraMBisu: \eng{we shall be ready to join
issue with them on this very point} nAvu avaroDane I aMshada meVleyeV
vAda mADalu sidadhx.
 
\alnum{b} (\nAyxshA) vivAdAMshavanunx tiVpiRge oTATxgi opipxsu. 
 
\alnum{c} (\nAyxshA) (oMdu pakaSx) matotxMdu pakaSx opipxsida vAdAMshavanunx aMgiVkarisu. 
\num{7} \eng{make an issue of} doDaDx raMpa mADu; rAdAdhxMta mADu; vAdaviSayavAgi mADu. 
\num{8} \eng{take issue}= \hyperlink{issue1 pagu6}{\pagu $(6)$}.}}

\pron{iTf}
\gl{\sanA}
{\dictmeaning{(SaSiThxV viBakitx \eng{its}; \bava\ \eng{they}, divxtiVyA viBakitx \eng{them}, SaSiThxV viBakitx \eng{their}). 
\num{1} adu; idu; parxsakatx viSaya, vasutx (kelavomemx liMga tiLiyada yA liMga aBiperxVtavAgirada pArxNi yA magu): \eng{took a stone and threw it} oMdu kalulx tegedukoMDu adanunx eseda. 
\num{2} parxsutxta vayxkitx: \eng{who is it that knocks?} adu yAru, bAgilu taTuTxvavanu? 
\eng{it is I} (adu) nAnu. \eng{is it a boy or a girl?} adu huDuganoV, huDugiyoV? 
\num{3} (\pArxparx, \kAparx) manasasxnunx vAyxpisiruvudu, tuMbiruvudu: \eng{it is the miller's daughter} giraNi mAlikana magaLu nananx manasasxnunx vAyxpisidAdxLe. 
\num{4} BAvavAcaka kirxyApadagaLa kataqRvAgi: \eng{it rains} maLe hoyuyxtatxde. \eng{it is cold} taNaNxgide. \eng{it is winter} (adu, idu) caLigAla. \eng{it is 6 miles to the village} haLiLxge Aru meYli (dUra) Agutatxde. \eng{it is Wednesday today} iMdu budhavAra. \eng{it says in the Bible} beYbalf ( -- eMdu) heVLutatxde. \eng{I would go if it were not for the expense} vecacxvilalxdidadxre nAnu hoVgutitxdedx. 
\num{5} muMde baruva nijavAda kataqRvanunx pUvaRBAviyAgi sUcisuva gwNa kataqRvAgi: \eng{it is absurd talking (to talk) like that} hAge mAtADuvudu asaMgata. \eng{it is incredible that he should refuse} avanu nirAkarisidaneMbudu naMbalu asAdhayx. 
\num{6} (\kirxvi\ AKAyxtadiMda parxteyxVkagoMDiruva, \eng{that} eMba saMbaMdhAvayxyadiMda pArxraMBavAgi muMde baruva kataqRvanunx pUvaRBAviyAgi sUcisuva): \eng{it is seldom that he fails} avanu tapipxsikoLuLxvudu viraLa. 
\num{7} (\eng{that} eMba) saMbaMdhAvayxyadiMda pArxraMBavAgi muMde baruva kamaRpadavanunx pUvaRBAviyAgi sUcisuva padavAgi: \eng{see to it that they obey} avaru pAlisuvaMte noVDiko. \eng{I take it that you agree} niVnu samamxtisutitxVyeMdu nAnu garxhisutetxVne. 
\num{8} (saMbaMdhasUcakakekx pUvaRgAmi padavAgi): \eng{it was a purse that he dropped} avanu biVLisidudx oMdu haNada ciVla. 
\num{9} (\sakirx\ yA \akirx doDane anideRVshaka kamaRpadavAgi) \eng{face it out} dheYyaRdiMda edurisu. \eng{carry it with a high hand} dapaRdiMda sAdhisu. \eng{deuce take it} adu hALAgali. \eng{run for it} tavxre mADu. \eng{lord it over him} avana meVle adhikAra naDesu. \eng{cab it} (rUDhiyAgi yA nidiRSaTx saMdaBaRdalilx) kAyxbf baMDiyalilx hoVgu. \eng{give it him (hot)} bisimuTiTxsu. \eng{have done it} aviveVka mADide. 
\num{10} (\AmA) sAdhane \mo vugaLa tutatxtudi; shiKara; paramAvadhi: \eng{for barefaced lying you really are it} nAcikeyilalxde suLuLx heVLuvudaralilx niVnu nijavAgi nisisxVma, tutatxtudi muTiTxdidxVye. 
\num{11} (\AmA) leYMgika AkaSaRNe yA saMBoVga. 
\num{12} (makakxLa ATagaLalilx) itararanunx hiDiyabeVkAda ATagAra.}}

\bentry
\word[hyp-ite(1)]{-ite}
\pron{-aiTf}
\gl{\uparx}
{\dictmeaning{nAmapadagaLanunx rUpisuva \uparx 
\num{1} vayxkitxgaLa hesarugaLalilx: 
 
\alnum{a} oMdu deVshada nivAsigaLu eMba athaRdalilx: \eng{Israelite}. 
 
\alnum{b} (\hiV) oMdu paMthada anuyAyigaLu eMbathaRdalilx: \eng{Benthamite, Pre-Raphaelite, Trotskyite}. 
\num{2} vasutxgaLa hesarugaLalilx: 
 
\alnum{a} paLeyuLike jiVvigaLa hesarugaLalilx: \eng{ammonite}. 
 
\alnum{b} Kanija jAtigaLa hesarugaLalilx: \eng{graphite, anthracite, haematite}. 
 
\alnum{c} deVhada yA aMgada GaTaka BAgagaLa hesarugaLalilx: \eng{somite} kAyaKaMDa. \eng{corite} shaqMgaKaMDa. 
 
\alnum{d} soPxVTakagaLa hesarugaLalilx: \eng{dynamite}. 
 
\alnum{e} vANijayx utapxnanxgaLa hesarugaLalilx: \eng{ebonite, vulcanite}. 
 
\alnum{f} Amalx lavaNagaLa hesarugaLalilx: \eng{nitrite, sulphite}. 
\num{3} kelavu sakakxreyuLaLx padAthaRgaLu, gUlxkoVsf, \mo\
hesarugaLalilx: \eng{dulcite, pinite}.}}

\bentry
\word[hyp-ite(2)]{-ite}
\pron{-aiTf}
\gl{\uparx}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} guNavAcakagaLanunx rUpisuva \uparx: \eng{erudite, composite,

\num{1} hAge, aMte, A riVti -- mADu yA Agu: \eng{Americanize,
dramatize, pulverize, realize}.
\num{2} A, aMtha parxkirxyege oLapaDisu: \eng{monopolize, pasteurize}. 
\num{3} (oMdu) nidiRSaTx vayxvasethxyanunx anusarisu: \eng{economize}. 
\num{4} (oMdu) nidiRSaTx BAva, BAvane hoMdiru: \eng{sympathize}. 
\num{5} tuMbu, odagisu yA (oMdara) pariNAmakekx, parxBAvakekx --
gurimADu, oLapaDisu: \eng{oxidize}.
\num{6} (oMdaralilx) iDu; irisu: \eng{containerize, hospitalize}. 
\num{7} (oMdara guNagaLiruvaMte) vatiRsu yA naDeduko: \eng{criticize,
deputize}.
\num{8} (nidiRSaTx vayxkitxya) parxkirxyeyanunx anusarisu; adara
parxkAra mADu, vatiRsu: \eng{bowdlerize}.}
\eentry

\bentry

\pron{-aisaZrf}
\gl{\uparx}
\dictmeaning{\nA\ \eng{-ise, -ize} aMtayxda \kirx gaLiMda kataqRvAcaka
nAmapadagaLanunx racisuvalilx baLasuva \uparx: \eng{civilizer}.}
\eentry
